<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="English">English</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: English"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><figure class="mw-halign-none" typeof="mw:File"><span><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/44px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="40" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/66px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/88px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94"></span><figcaption></figcaption></figure></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">English <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="en"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/durian" class="extiw" title="w:durian">durian</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/durian" class="extiw" title="w:durian">Wikipedia </a></span></div>
<figure class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Durio_kutej_F_070203_ime.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9a/Durio_kutej_F_070203_ime.jpg/220px-Durio_kutej_F_070203_ime.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="167" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9a/Durio_kutej_F_070203_ime.jpg/330px-Durio_kutej_F_070203_ime.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/9/9a/Durio_kutej_F_070203_ime.jpg 2x" data-file-width="422" data-file-height="320"></a><figcaption>Durian fruits</figcaption></figure>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Malay">durian</a></i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Austronesian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Austronesian language">Proto-Austronesian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="map-pro"><a href="/wiki/Reconstruction:Proto-Austronesian/du%CA%80i" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Austronesian/duʀi">*duʀi</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thorn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#doublet" title="Appendix:Glossary">Doublet</a> of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/iwi#English" title="iwi">iwi</a></i>, from Māori.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Pronunciation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/British_English" class="extiw" title="w:British English">UK</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˈdʊə.ɹɪən/</span>, <span class="IPA">/ˈdʒʊə.ɹɪən/</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/American_English" class="extiw" title="w:American English">US</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href="/wiki/Wiktionary:International_Phonetic_Alphabet" title="Wiktionary:International Phonetic Alphabet">IPA</a><sup>(<a href="/wiki/Appendix:English_pronunciation" title="Appendix:English pronunciation">key</a>)</sup>: <span class="IPA">/ˈdʊə.ɹi.ən/</span>, <span class="IPA">/ˈdʊə.ɹiˌɑn/</span></li></ul>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><span class="headword-line"><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en">durian</strong> (<i><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#countable" title="Appendix:Glossary">countable</a> and <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href="/wiki/durians#English" title="durians">durians</a></b>)</span>
</p>
<ol><li>Any of several <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/tree#English" title="tree">trees</a>, <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/genus#English" title="genus">genus</a> <i><a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Durio#English" title="Durio">Durio</a></i>, of <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/Southeast_Asia#English" title="Southeast Asia">Southeast Asia</a>.</li>
<li>The <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/spiky#English" title="spiky">spiky</a> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/edible#English" title="edible">edible</a> <a href="/wiki/fruit#Noun" title="fruit">fruit</a> of this tree, known for its <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/strong#English" title="strong">strong</a> <a href="/wiki/taste#Noun" title="taste">taste</a> and very strong, <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/unpleasant#English" title="unpleasant">unpleasant</a> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/odor#English" title="odor">odor</a>.
<span class="HQToggle" style="margin-left: 5px;"><a role="button" tabindex="0">quotations&nbsp;▼</a></span><ul style="display: none;"><li><b>1692</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Robert_Boyle" class="extiw" title="w:Robert Boyle">Robert Boyle</a>, <i>General Heads for the Natural History of a Country Great or Small,</i> London: John Taylor and S. Hedford, “Enquiries for <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_Suratte" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch Suratte">Suratte</a>, &amp;c.,” p.&nbsp;96,<sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://name.umdl.umich.edu/A28984.0001.001">[1]</a></sup>
<dl><dd>Whether the <i><a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/betel#English" title="betel">Betele</a></i> hath such a contrariety to the <i><b>Durion</b></i>, that a few Leaves of that, put to a whole Shopful of <i><b>Durions</b></i>, will make them all rot suddenly; and whether those that have surfeited on <i><b>Durions</b></i>, and thereby over-heated themselves, do, by laying a Leaf or two of <i>Betele</i> upon their Breasts or Stomachs, immediately cure the Inflammations, and Recover.</dd></dl></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>1869</b></span> November, “The Land of the Malay: A Record of Travel in the Oriental Tropics”, in <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Thomas_Mayne_Reid" class="extiw" title="w:Thomas Mayne Reid">[Thomas] Mayne Reid</a>, editor, <cite>Onward: A Magazine for the Young Manhood of America</cite>, New York, N.Y.: Onward Publishing Office, <small><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://www.worldcat.org/title/8717398">→OCLC</a></small>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=nQ7ZAAAAMAAJ&amp;pg=PA494">page <span class="None" lang="und">494</span></a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">The dessert I thoroughly enjoyed, for the various fruits of Singapore are delicious. One of them, the "<b>durion</b>," exhales a most noxious perfume, but is pleasant to the palate.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><span class="None" lang="und"><b>1956</b></span>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anthony_Burgess" class="extiw" title="w:Anthony Burgess">Anthony Burgess</a>, <cite>Time for a Tiger</cite> (The Malayan Trilogy), published <span class="None" lang="und">1972</span>, page <span class="None" lang="und">115</span>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation cited-passage" lang="en">Old women crouched over bags of Siamese rice, skeps of red and green peppers, purple egg-plants, bristly rambutans, pineapples, <b>durians</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="usage-label-sense"><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#uncountable" title="Appendix:Glossary">uncountable</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span></span> A deep, rich <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/yellow#English" title="yellow">yellow</a> <a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/colour#English" title="colour">colour</a>, like that of durian flesh (also called durian yellow).
<dl><dd><div class="color-panel">durian: <span style="background-color:#E1BD27; display:inline-block; width:80px;">&nbsp;</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Alternative_forms">Alternative forms</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Alternative forms"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Brunei_Malay">Brunei Malay</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Brunei Malay"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="kxd"><a href="/wiki/duri#Brunei_Malay" title="duri">duri</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thorn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> +‎ <i class="Latn mention" lang="kxd"><a href="/wiki/-an#Brunei_Malay" title="-an">-an</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Malayic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Malayic language">Proto-Malayic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="poz-mly-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Malayic/duri-an&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Malayic/duri-an (page does not exist)">*duri-an</a></i>, from (Western) <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Malayo-Polynesian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian language">Proto-Malayo-Polynesian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="poz-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian/du%CA%80i-an&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian/duʀi-an (page does not exist)">*duʀi-an</a></i>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Danish">Danish</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Danish"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><figure class="mw-halign-none" typeof="mw:File"><span><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/44px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="40" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/66px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/88px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94"></span><figcaption></figcaption></figure></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">Danish <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="da"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/da:durian" class="extiw" title="w:da:durian">durian</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/da:durian" class="extiw" title="w:da:durian">Wikipedia <sup>da</sup></a></span></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_6">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#English">durian</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Malay">durian</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Malayic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Malayic language">Proto-Malayic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="poz-mly-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Malayic/duri-an&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Malayic/duri-an (page does not exist)">*duri-an</a></i>, from (Western) <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Malayo-Polynesian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian language">Proto-Malayo-Polynesian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="poz-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian/du%CA%80i-an&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian/duʀi-an (page does not exist)">*duʀi-an</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_7">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="French">French</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: French"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><figure class="mw-halign-none" typeof="mw:File"><span><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/44px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="40" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/66px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/88px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94"></span><figcaption></figcaption></figure></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">French <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="fr"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/fr:durian" class="extiw" title="w:fr:durian">durian</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/fr:durian" class="extiw" title="w:fr:durian">Wikipedia <sup>fr</sup></a></span></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_7">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=30" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#English">durian</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Malay">durian</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Malayic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Malayic language">Proto-Malayic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="poz-mly-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Malayic/duri-an&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Malayic/duri-an (page does not exist)">*duri-an</a></i>, from (Western) <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Malayo-Polynesian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian language">Proto-Malayo-Polynesian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="poz-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian/du%CA%80i-an&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian/duʀi-an (page does not exist)">*duʀi-an</a></i>.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_8">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Indonesian">Indonesian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Indonesian"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><figure class="mw-halign-none" typeof="mw:File"><span><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/44px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="40" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/66px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/88px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94"></span><figcaption></figcaption></figure></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">Indonesian <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="id"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/id:durian" class="extiw" title="w:id:durian">durian</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/id:durian" class="extiw" title="w:id:durian">Wikipedia <sup>id</sup></a></span></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_8">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Reconstructed as <i class="Latn mention" lang="id"><a href="/wiki/duri#Indonesian" title="duri">duri</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thorn, spike</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> +‎ <i class="Latn mention" lang="id"><a href="/wiki/-an#Indonesian" title="-an">-an</a></i>, <a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#inherited" title="Appendix:Glossary">inherited</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Malay">durian</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Malayic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Malayic language">Proto-Malayic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="poz-mly-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Malayic/duri-an&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Malayic/duri-an (page does not exist)">*duri-an</a></i>, from (Western) <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Malayo-Polynesian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian language">Proto-Malayo-Polynesian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="poz-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian/du%CA%80i-an&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian/duʀi-an (page does not exist)">*duʀi-an</a></i>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Italian">Italian</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=40" title="Edit section: Italian"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><figure class="mw-halign-none" typeof="mw:File"><span><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/44px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="40" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/66px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/88px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94"></span><figcaption></figcaption></figure></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">Italian <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="it"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/it:durian" class="extiw" title="w:it:durian">durian</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/it:durian" class="extiw" title="w:it:durian">Wikipedia <sup>it</sup></a></span></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_9">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=41" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#English">durian</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Malay">durian</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Malayic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Malayic language">Proto-Malayic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="poz-mly-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Malayic/duri-an&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Malayic/duri-an (page does not exist)">*duri-an</a></i>, from (Western) <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Malayo-Polynesian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian language">Proto-Malayo-Polynesian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="poz-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian/du%CA%80i-an&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian/duʀi-an (page does not exist)">*duʀi-an</a></i>.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_10">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=45" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Malay">Malay</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=47" title="Edit section: Malay"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><figure class="mw-halign-none" typeof="mw:File"><span><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/44px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="40" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/66px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/88px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94"></span><figcaption></figcaption></figure></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">Malay <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="ms"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ms:durian" class="extiw" title="w:ms:durian">durian</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ms:durian" class="extiw" title="w:ms:durian">Wikipedia <sup>ms</sup></a></span></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_11">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=48" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="ms"><a href="/wiki/duri#Malay" title="duri">duri</a></i> +‎ <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms"><a href="/wiki/-an#Malay" title="-an">-an</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Malayic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Malayic language">Proto-Malayic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="poz-mly-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Malayic/duri-an&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Malayic/duri-an (page does not exist)">*duri-an</a></i>, from (Western) <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Malayo-Polynesian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian language">Proto-Malayo-Polynesian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="poz-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian/du%CA%80i-an&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian/duʀi-an (page does not exist)">*duʀi-an</a></i>.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_12">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=50" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

</p>

<h2><span id="Norwegian_Bokm.C3.A5l"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Norwegian_Bokmål">Norwegian Bokmål</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=53" title="Edit section: Norwegian Bokmål"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><figure class="mw-halign-none" typeof="mw:File"><span><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/44px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="40" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/66px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/88px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94"></span><figcaption></figcaption></figure></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">Norwegian <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="no"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/no:durian" class="extiw" title="w:no:durian">durian</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/no:durian" class="extiw" title="w:no:durian">Wikipedia <sup>no</sup></a></span></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_12">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=54" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#English">durian</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Malay">durian</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Malayic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Malayic language">Proto-Malayic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="poz-mly-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Malayic/duri-an&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Malayic/duri-an (page does not exist)">*duri-an</a></i>, from (Western) <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Malayo-Polynesian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian language">Proto-Malayo-Polynesian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="poz-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian/du%CA%80i-an&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian/duʀi-an (page does not exist)">*duʀi-an</a></i>.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_13">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=55" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_13">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=57" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p><a href="/wiki/Appendix:Glossary#loanword" title="Appendix:Glossary">Borrowed</a> from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#English">durian</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Malay">durian</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Malayic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Malayic language">Proto-Malayic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="poz-mly-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Malayic/duri-an&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Malayic/duri-an (page does not exist)">*duri-an</a></i>, from (Western) <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Malayo-Polynesian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian language">Proto-Malayo-Polynesian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="poz-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian/du%CA%80i-an&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian/duʀi-an (page does not exist)">*duʀi-an</a></i>.
</p>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_14">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=63" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#English">durian</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Malay">durian</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Malayic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Malayic language">Proto-Malayic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="poz-mly-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Malayic/duri-an&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Malayic/duri-an (page does not exist)">*duri-an</a></i>, from (Western) <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Malayo-Polynesian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian language">Proto-Malayo-Polynesian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="poz-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian/du%CA%80i-an&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian/duʀi-an (page does not exist)">*duʀi-an</a></i>.
</p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Tagalog">Tagalog</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=66" title="Edit section: Tagalog"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronunciation_8">Pronunciation</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=67" title="Edit section: Pronunciation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_16">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=68" title="Edit section: Noun"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Turkish">Turkish</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=69" title="Edit section: Turkish"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="sister-wikipedia sister-project noprint floatright" style="border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background: #f9f9f9; width: 250px; padding: 4px; text-align: left;"><div style="float: left;"><figure class="mw-halign-none" typeof="mw:File"><span><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/44px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="44" height="40" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/66px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/80/Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg/88px-Wikipedia-logo-v2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="103" data-file-height="94"></span><figcaption></figcaption></figure></div><div style="margin-left: 60px;">Turkish <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia" title="Wikipedia">Wikipedia</a> has an article on:<div style="margin-left: 10px;"><b class="Latn" lang="tr"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/tr:durian" class="extiw" title="w:tr:durian">durian</a></b></div></div><span class="interProject"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/tr:durian" class="extiw" title="w:tr:durian">Wikipedia <sup>tr</sup></a></span></div>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_15">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=durian&amp;action=edit&amp;section=70" title="Edit section: Etymology"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#English">durian</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Malay_language" class="extiw" title="w:Malay language">Malay</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="ms"><a class="mw-selflink-fragment" href="#Malay">durian</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Malayic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Malayic language">Proto-Malayic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="poz-mly-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Malayic/duri-an&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Malayic/duri-an (page does not exist)">*duri-an</a></i>, from (Western) <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Malayo-Polynesian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian language">Proto-Malayo-Polynesian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="poz-pro"><a href="/w/index.php?title=Reconstruction:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian/du%CA%80i-an&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Reconstruction:Proto-Malayo-Polynesian/duʀi-an (page does not exist)">*duʀi-an</a></i>.
</p>
